09/01/26, 7:01 pm - Vishnu Broski: *Q1) Data Science in Healthcare* 
Data science in healthcare uses data analysis, machine learning, and statistics to improve diagnosis, treatment, and patient care.
Applications:
Disease prediction (diabetes, cancer, heart disease)
Medical image analysis (X-ray, MRI, skin disease detection)
Patient monitoring using wearable devices
Personalized treatment plans
Hospital resource management
Benefits:
Early disease detection
Better decision-making for doctors
Reduced healthcare cost
Improved patient outcomes
Example:
Analyzing patient history and lab reports to predict disease risk.
 *Q2) Transformation of E-Commerce with Data Science* 
Data science has transformed e-commerce by improving customer experience, sales, and business efficiency.
Key Transformations:
Recommendation systems (products based on user interest)
Customer behavior analysis
Dynamic pricing
Fraud detection
Inventory and supply chain optimization
Benefits:
Increased sales and customer satisfaction
Personalized shopping experience
Reduced fraud and returns
Better demand forecasting
Example:
Amazon recommending products based on previous searches and purchases.
 *Q3) Weather Prediction Using Data Science* 
Data science helps in accurate weather forecasting by analyzing large amounts of historical and real-time data.
Data Used:
Temperature
Humidity
Wind speed
Satellite images
Atmospheric pressure
Process:
Collect weather data
Clean and preprocess data
Analyze patterns
Apply machine learning models
Predict future weather conditions
Applications:
Agriculture planning
Disaster management
Aviation and transport
Climate change analysis
Example:
Predicting rainfall to help farmers plan irrigation <This message was edited>

12/03/26, 12:52 pm - Bharath: Hi, 
I’m Bharath, a BTech CSE student at VIT with a build real products mindset. I’ve always been more interested in creating real world products than following tutorials, I believe code only matters if it provides some value to an end user in some way or the other.

My recent project, **TypeScout** was based on this mindset. It’s a web scraping tool that identifies and previews fonts on any website, allowing users to download them instantly. While I initially built it to satisfy my own obsession with **clean UI/UX**, it quickly became quite popular among my peers as a useful utility. I’m coming to this hackathon to get my hands dirty, build something from scratch, and solve another real world problem with a high quality frontend and robust logic.

***(Screenshots of TypeScout)***

![image](https://assets.devfolio.co/content/4fd4bf4fd5214c7f8036e92da813e4ba/0efa535b-1dce-44cd-909d-9bb6c0e6f55a.png)

![image](https://assets.devfolio.co/content/4fd4bf4fd5214c7f8036e92da813e4ba/4cf344cf-f376-44a3-b70d-88507b407ee3.png)

Apart from TypeScout, I’ve also built **ZenNotes**, a React-based offline note-taker that focuses on a distraction free experience. Right now, I’m building a **P2P based offline chat window.** The idea is to enable communication over a local network during emergencies like natural disasters where the internet isn't an option.

Anyways I’d love the chance to show what I can build over the weekend if I get the opportunity to be there: )

Thankyou for considering my application!
